<li>The supplying of goods, wares, merchandise, etc.</li></ol>

***levertraan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:levertraan.html>levertraan</a> (74699)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lever.html>lever</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">liver</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:traan.html>traan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fish oil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:levertraan.html>levertraan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cod liver oil</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a widespread misconception in Belgium and the Netherlands that <i><a href = vnd.unilang:levertraan.html>levertraan</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> actually made from whale livers, affecting use of the term. (Compare the same in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Lebertran</i>.) When stating that one uses <i><a href = vnd.unilang:levertraan.html>levertraan</a></i> it may therefore be advised to clarify it does not contain whale livers, as whaling <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unpopular in both countries.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">walvistraan</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:levertraan.html>levertraan</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dierlijke.html>dierlijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:olie.html>olie</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gewonnen.html>gewonnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lever.html>lever</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kabeljauw.html>kabeljauw</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:schelvis.html>schelvis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vissen.html>vissen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:familie.html>familie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schelvis.html>schelvissen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <i>Gadidae</i></li></ol>

***lezen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lezen.html>lezen</a> (738)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lēsen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to collect, gather, read</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lesan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to gather, read</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lesaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to gather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*les-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to gather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lezen.html>lezen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to read
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lees.html>lees</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:graag.html>graag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boeken.html>boeken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I like to <b>read</b> books.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:binnen.html>binnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begon.html>begon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwe.html>nieuwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lezen.html>lezen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> in and started to <b>read</b> his new book.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gather (esp. fruits)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">(...) <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> mogten in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemeente.html>gemeente</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vruchten.html>vruchten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lezen.html>lezen</a> (...)</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div> (1834, Afscheidsrede <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> s̕ Gravenhage, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.be/books?id=KRliAAAAcAAJamp;pg=PA14amp;lpg=PA14amp;dq=%22vruchten+lezen%22amp;source=blamp;ots=JSMQvx3fxsamp;sig=ACfU3U34g1RsARuHx8B3EG_HESDPTwn7mwamp;hl=nlamp;sa=Xamp;ved=2ahUKEwi40qf0sI_nAhWGL1AKHRzAB7UQ6AEwAHoECAsQAQv=onepageamp;q=%22vruchten%20lezen%22amp;f=false">[1]</a>)</dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lezer.html>lezer</a> (17823)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lesere</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lezen.html>lezen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to read</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lezer.html>lezer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lezers.html>lezers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lezer.html>lezertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A reader, person who reads a text</li>
<li>A reader, device to read one or more <a href = vnd.unilang:parameters.html>parameters</a>, often numerically expressed, or a whole encrypted (e.g. audio-visual) file</li></ol>

***lezing.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lezing.html>lezing</a> (6613)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lesinge</i>. <p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">libertin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">libertīnus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:libertijn.html>libertijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:libertijnen.html>libertijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:libertijn.html>libertijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">libertine</span>, one who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> loose morals.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A religious dissenter who didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> adhere to Protestant (usually Reformed) orthodoxy; often used of Anabaptists, more loosely also of Remonstrants.</li></ol>

***licentie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:licentie.html>licentie</a> (17646)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">licence</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">licentia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">license</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">licens</i>, present participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">licere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be allowed, be allowable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">linquere</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λείπω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">leípō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">leave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***licht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a> (765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*līht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*linhtaz</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁lengʷʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lichter.html>lichter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lichtst.html>lichtst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>light, of little weight</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> easy, mild</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lieht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*leuht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*leuhtą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lewk-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">light; bright; to shine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lichten.html>lichten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lichtje.html>lichtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A light, illumination</li>
<li>A light source</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> inspiration (in <i>z'n <a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opsteken.html>opsteken</a></i>); a bright mind
<ul><li><b>1992</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A._F._Th._van_der_Heijden" class="extiw" title="w:A. F. Th. van der Heijden">A. F. Th. <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Heijden</a>, <i>Weerborstels</i>, Em. Querido's <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeverij.html>Uitgeverij</a>, page 52:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>Geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>groot</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> Bossche voddendief, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ermee.html>ermee</a>.
<dl><dd>No genius, that rag thief from Den <a href = vnd.unilang:bosch.html>Bosch</a>, but I made do with it.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lieht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*leuht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*leuhtaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lewk-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">light; bright; to shine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lichter.html>lichter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lichtst.html>lichtst</a></b>)

***lid.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a> (1871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">let</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">leet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*liþuz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leden.html>leden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lidje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">ledeken</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">member</span> (of a group)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lidmaat.html>lidmaat</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">member</span>, limb (extremity of a body)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ledemaat.html>ledemaat</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>member, <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> article, <span class="use-with-mention">particularly in the Southern diminutive form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ledeken</i></span> <span class="defdate">[from late 16th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lidwoord.html>lidwoord</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">voorlid</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">let</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hlidą</i>.
</p>

***lied.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lied.html>lied</a> (2679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:liet.html>liet</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lioth</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*leuþą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lied.html>lied</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liederen.html>liederen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liedje.html>liedje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>song</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The plural <i><a href = vnd.unilang:liederen.html>liederen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now chiefly restricted to solemn <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>songs</a>, such as hymns or anthems. Otherwise the plural diminutive <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liedjes.html>liedjes</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used. (The singular <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also more often than not replaced with <i><a href = vnd.unilang:liedje.html>liedje</a></i> when referring to a “mundane” song.)
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:lied.html>lied</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:muziek.html>muziek</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:muzikale.html>muzikale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorm.html>vorm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarin.html>waarin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tekst.html>tekst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muziek.html>muziek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> verklankt, <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> vormgegeven in <a href = vnd.unilang:couplet.html>couplet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:refrein.html>refrein</a>
<dl><dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sleuren.html>sleurde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:abt.html>abt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haren.html>haren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:smalle.html>smalle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:smeet.html>smeet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vloer.html>vloer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sloeg.html>sloeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> roe <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:raken.html>raken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zingen.html>zingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lied.html>lied</a></b> '<a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a> Pastor Alterne'.</i><sup id="cite_ref-Het_hele_jaar_rond:_van_Sinterklaas_tot_Sintemaarten,_p._14_2-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Het_hele_jaar_rond:_van_Sinterklaas_tot_Sintemaarten,_p._14-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></dd></dl></li></ol>

***lieden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lieden.html>lieden</a> (15795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">liede</i>, originally a singular collective noun. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*liudi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*liudiz</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lout</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lede.html>lede</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">leod</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:leed.html>leed</a></i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Leute</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lieden.html>lieden</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>; people</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:lieden.html>lieden</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">mv</span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>

</p>

***liefdadig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:liefdadig.html>liefdadig</a> (56869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lief.html>lief</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">love</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daad.html>daad</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liefdadig.html>liefdadig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liefdadig.html>liefdadiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">liefdadigst</b>)
